style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Smartavillas
Unipessoal Lda (hereafter referred to as Smartavillas) </span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>is
a Portuguese Registered property management company acting on behalf of the
property owner. The Agreement to rent is made between the guest and the
property owner.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>In</span><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'> making a booking, the first named person on the booking
information agrees on behalf of all persons within the booking party that:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>•	A contract between you and the property owner will come into existence when payment is received and will be deemed as of acceptance of these Terms and Conditions. The contract binds you & all the members of your party and It is your responsibility to ensure that all members of your party accept the prescribed terms. Failure to disclose all relevant information or comply with these terms may lead to termination of the contract & loss of the booking. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>•	Bookings cannot be accepted from persons under eighteen years of age.</span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>•	You consent to our use of your information in accordance with our Privacy Notice and in accordance with local laws.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>•	These Booking Conditions and any agreement to which they apply are governed in all respects by Portuguese law.  We both agree that any dispute, claim or other matter which arises between us out of or in connection with your contract or booking will be dealt with by Binding Arbitration under Portuguese Law.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>a)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Guest Occupancy - </span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>No parties or events - the maximum number of persons using the accommodation
at any time must not exceed&nbsp;the maximum occupancy and only those listed on
the booking form can occupy the property. We reserve the right to terminate the
booking without notice and without refund in case of a breach of this
condition.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>b)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Smoking</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'> </span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>- Smoking or v</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>aping anywhere inside the premises is not permitted and could
result termination of occupancy and forfeiture of all Security Deposits. This
must be strictly adhered to and any damage or extra cleaning caused by smoking
will be at your own expense. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>c)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Pets</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'> (<em><span style='font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>if not
allowed</span></em>) brought to and staying inside the premises will result in
immediate termination of occupancy and forfeiture of all payments. This must be
strictly adhered to and any damage or extra cleaning caused by pets or smoking
will be at your own expense. For properties allowing pets, an additional fee
will be charged. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>d)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>On Departure - </span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>The accommodation should be left in an acceptable condition to
enable it to be sufficiently prepared for the next guests. This includes proper
<a name='_Hlk35979680'>disposal of waste and rubbish items which should be
disposed of in the nearby containers or recycling points, and not left inside the
property or within the grounds of the property. We also ask that the BBQ is
left in a good condition without wasted charcoal or food debris, as this will
attract vermin. </a></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>The property owner reserves
the right to make a charge to cover additional cleaning costs if the client
leaves the property in an unacceptable condition.</span><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> Please
note that if any keys issued are not returned at the end of your stay, then the
cost of replacement will be charged to you.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>e)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>SEF Reporting</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'> - By law, </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>we must
report all non-Portuguese citizens that stay in Portuguese rental accommodation
to <b>SEF</b> (Serviço de Estrangeiros e Fronteiras). It is therefore
imperative that we have all passport details. We will ask for these details at <b><u>the
time of booking</u></b>, to complete the reservation. If any guests' passports
are unavailable as they are being renewed, please be aware that they will be required
and need to be supplied as soon as possible and certainly no later than your
arrival at the accommo</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>dation.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span

</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:

line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> - All
bookings are subject to a non-refundable booking fee.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>c)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Security and Damages Deposits:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Smartavillas operates 2 policies in respect of Security and Damages
Deposits, and you will be informed at the time of booking which applies to your
booking.</span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=i>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:black;margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;
     background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
     115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Apartments, Townhouses and
     Small Villas</span></b></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Smaller and Medium sized properties are subject to a <b>non-refundable
Accidental Damage Waiver </b>which is included in the booking fee. This is
aimed to insure guests against accidental damage to the property up to a value
of 250€ per booking but excludes negligence or vandalism. For any damage that
exceeds 250€, Smartavillas reserves the right to invoice you for immediate payment.</span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=2 type=i>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:
     white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
     font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Large Villas and
     Quintas</span></b></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>When booking our larger, exclusive villas a <b>refundable Security
Deposit of 500€</b> will be required. This should be paid upon arrival. The
return of this deposit will be subject to a satisfactory inspection and check
of the property following departure and will be returned with 14 days of the
leaving date. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang=EN-US

lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Additional Guests</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> -
</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>For properties with additional
sleeping facilities such as a spare occasional bed or a sofa bed, a charge of <b>10€
per person per night</b> will be levied. Additional guest sleeping facilities
will be listed in the facilities description. E.g., A 2-bedroom property may
accept 6 guests in the 2 bedrooms, plus 1 double sofa bed. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:

</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Late Night Check-in</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>
- Many of our properties have a key safety box. For properties without this
facility, a personal, late night check-in will be provided. The fees levied for
this service outside of normal hours will be according to the following times
and are payable upon arrival. </span></p>

</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;background:white'><b><span

background:white'>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white;border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span lang=EN-US

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>a)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span

will need to complete the required booking details<b> </b>to confirm your booking

information. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>b)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;

you book, you will receive a breakdown of all costings associated with the

balance.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>c)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Confirmation</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> - Once
the booking is confirmed we will send the full address of your rental property,
travel directions and other important information. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>d)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span

10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> -
We will contact you again to confirm your final travel arrangements, answer any
final questions you may have concerning your check in at your rental property. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'></span></p>

<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white;border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>4.<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>PAYING FOR THE BOOKING </span></b></p>

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Payment Terms</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>, including
changes and cancellations are outlined in <b>Appendix 1.</b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>a)<span
style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Payment Methods</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'> -
Payments are required in the nominated currency and must be paid according to
the schedule. Payments can be made in the following ways:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:normal'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>As
you will appreciate, sufficient time needs to be given to cleaning and preparing
the accommodation for your stay, as well as the incoming guests. We guarantee
that accommodation will be available after 4pm (16.00h) on the day of arrival
and request that it is vacated by 10am (10.00h) on the day of departure. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Of
course, we do understand that flight timetables and travel plans do not always
fall in line with this schedule and will do everything possible to assist with
earlier arrival and later departure times. For instance, if you are arriving
early, we may be able to arrange a bag drop whilst we complete the rental
property preparations. In the case of later departures, we will do our best to
assist with either a late checkout or luggage storage and recommendations of
nearby facilities, which may incur a charge. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>b)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Late Arrivals:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>In
some of our properties, key safe boxes are installed. In this instance, if you
are arriving late, we will supply you with the key safe code in advance and then
arrange a courtesy visit for the following day. If the property does not have
the key safe facility and we need to meet you with the keys, please remember
that there will be a charge for the late check in- payable on arrival to the representative,
as detailed in the relevant table in Section 2, point (e). </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><b><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

Further details available on request.</span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>b)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>Standards of Accommodation, Décor,
Furnishings and Appliances within the Rental Property </span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif'>We
endeavor to ensure that rental properties are well equipped with appliances
essential to a self-catering holiday accommodation, but this will vary between
properties. In addition, internal fixtures, fittings and furnishings are installed
to the owners' preferences and the standard and quality of which will also
vary. Of course, every property is different, and we therefore recommend that
you check with us beforehand if there is anything you specifically require.
The advertised interior/exterior photographs and descriptions are intended to
accurately represent the property and should not vary substantially. However, the
company does not accept any responsibility for items of furniture etc which
appear in photographs but may have been changed or removed, nor for any changes
to aspects or views since photographs were taken. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;

</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Accommodations are classified as Car Essential,
Car Recommended or Car Not Essential</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;

</span></span><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:

style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;

and other amenities.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;

style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;- there are a few amenities within walking distance,
although a car will be required to reach major amenities.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span

</span></span><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>•	Car Not Essential </span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;- the property is within walking distance of supermarkets or
minimarkets, shops, restaurants, and other amenities.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><b><span style='font-size:15.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;

font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>d)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Utilities - </span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Water, electricity and gas consumption are included within the
property's rental cost unless otherwise stated. Unfortunately, Portugal can sometimes
suffer from water or electricity shortages and supplies can be cut off without
notice for varying periods of time, which is outside our control. In addition,
you might find that the electricity may trip if too many appliances are used simultaneously.
You should contact us if you experience difficulties.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:15.0pt;

vertical-align:baseline'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>e)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Air conditioning/heating - </span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'>Not all properties have air conditioning installed. If you need
this facility, please check the accommodation description, and contact us if
you have any doubts. Some air conditioning units can also be reversed to
provide warmth. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:15.0pt;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>f)<span style='font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman''>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
'Century Gothic',sans-serif;color:black'>Winter Rentals</span></b><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:'Century Gothic',sans-serif;
color:black'> - For properties without air conditioning units which can provide
adequate heating, mobile radiators can be made available for your comfort during
the cooler months. Please note - For longer term winter lettings, the Gas,
Water and Electricity consumed by the occupier is usually an additional charge payable
monthly.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:15.0pt;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;

the start of the rental. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white'><span

refund of deposit payment </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span

<p class='MsoNormal' align='center' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:center'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:5.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' align='center' style='text-align:center'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Smartavillas Unipessoal Lda (doravante designada por Smartavillas)</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> é uma empresa portuguesa de gestão imobiliária que atua em nome do proprietário. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>O contrato de arrendamento é feito entre o hóspede e o proprietário do imóvel.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>1. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp; </span></span></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>CONDIÇÕES </font></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>DE </font></span></b></font><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>RESERVA</font></font></span></b></p>
</div>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Ao </font></font></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>fazer uma reserva, a primeira pessoa indicada nas informações de reserva concorda em nome de todas as pessoas da parte da reserva que:</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>• Um contrato entre você e o proprietário do imóvel entrará em vigor quando o pagamento for recebido e será considerado a partir da aceitação destes Termos e Condições. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>O contrato obriga você e todos os membros do seu partido e é sua responsabilidade garantir que todos os membros do seu partido aceitem os termos prescritos. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>A não divulgação de todas as informações relevantes ou o cumprimento destes termos pode levar à rescisão do contrato e perda da reserva.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>• Não podem ser aceitas reservas de pessoas menores de dezoito anos. </font></font></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>• Você consente com o uso de suas informações de acordo com nosso Aviso de Privacidade e de acordo com as leis locais.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;
vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>• Estas Condições de Reserva e qualquer acordo a que se apliquem são regidos em todos os aspectos pela lei portuguesa. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Ambos concordamos que qualquer disputa, reclamação ou outro assunto que surja entre nós devido ou em conexão com o seu contrato ou reserva será tratado por Arbitragem Vinculativa ao abrigo da Lei Portuguesa.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>a) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Ocupação dos hóspedes -</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> Sem festas ou eventos - o número máximo de pessoas que usam a acomodação a qualquer momento não deve exceder a ocupação máxima e apenas as listadas no formulário de reserva podem ocupar a propriedade. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Nós nos reservamos o direito de cancelar a reserva sem aviso prévio e sem reembolso em caso de violação desta condição.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>b) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Fumar</font></font></span></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Fumar ou v </font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>apitar em qualquer lugar dentro das instalações não é permitido e pode resultar na rescisão da ocupação e perda de todos os depósitos de segurança. </font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Isso deve ser estritamente observado e qualquer dano ou limpeza extra causado pelo fumo será de sua responsabilidade.</font></span></font><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'> </span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>c) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Animais de estimação</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> ( </font></font><em><span style='font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>se não permitidos</font></font></span></em><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> ) trazidos e permanecendo dentro das instalações resultarão na rescisão imediata da ocupação e perda de todos os pagamentos. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Isso deve ser estritamente observado e qualquer dano ou limpeza extra causado por animais de estimação ou fumo será de sua responsabilidade. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Para propriedades que permitem animais de estimação, uma taxa adicional será cobrada.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>d) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Na Saída -</font></font></span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> A acomodação deve ser deixada em condições aceitáveis &ZeroWidthSpace;&ZeroWidthSpace;para que esteja suficientemente preparada para os próximos hóspedes. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Isso inclui o </font></font><a name='_Hlk35979680'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>descarte</font></font></a></span><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> adequado
 </font></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><a name='_Hlk35979680'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>de resíduos e itens de lixo que devem ser descartados em recipientes próximos ou pontos de reciclagem, e não deixados dentro da propriedade ou no terreno da propriedade. </font></a></span><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><a name='_Hlk35979680'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Também pedimos que a churrasqueira seja deixada em boas condições, sem desperdício de carvão ou restos de comida, pois isso atrairá vermes. </font></a></span></font><span style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>O proprietário do imóvel reserva-se o direito de cobrar custos adicionais de limpeza caso o cliente deixe o imóvel em condições inaceitáveis. </font></font></span><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por favor, observe que se as chaves emitidas não forem devolvidas no final da sua estadia, o custo de substituição será cobrado de você.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>e) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Notificação do SEF</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Por lei, </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>devemos comunicar ao </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>SEF</font></font></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> todos os cidadãos não portugueses que se hospedem em alojamento para aluguer em Portugal </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Portanto, é fundamental que tenhamos todos os detalhes do passaporte. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Solicitaremos esses dados no </font></font><b><u><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>momento da reserva</font></font></u></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> , para finalizar a reserva. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Se os passaportes de algum hóspede não estiverem disponíveis durante a renovação, por favor, esteja ciente de que eles serão solicitados e precisam ser fornecidos o mais rápido possível e certamente o mais tardar em sua chegada ao alojamento </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;line-height:normal'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;line-height:normal'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;border:none;padding:
0cm'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>2. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black;background:white'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>PREÇOS DE ALUGUEL E </font></font></span></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>TAXAS </font></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black;background:white'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>ADICIONAIS</font></span></b></font><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'></font></span></b></p>
</div>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>O objetivo do Smartavillas é ser totalmente transparente </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>sobre quais taxas ou encargos extras podem ser cobrados. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Todos os itens adicionais estão listados abaixo, por favor, não hesite em buscar esclarecimentos sobre qualquer aspecto.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:5.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>a) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Tarifas de arrendamento -</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> Todas as tarifas
 </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>são anunciadas em € Euros, por noite, e o custo total da sua reserva, de acordo com as noites pretendidas, estará claramente visível.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>b) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Taxa de reserva</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Todas as reservas estão sujeitas a uma taxa de reserva não reembolsável.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>c) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Cauções e Cauções:</font></font></span></b></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Smartavillas opera 2 políticas em relação à Segurança e Depósitos de Danos, e você será informado no momento da reserva, o que se aplica à sua reserva.</font></font></span></p>
<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start='1' type='i'>
 <li class='MsoNormal' style='color:black;margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;
     background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
     115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Apartamentos, moradias geminadas e pequenas vilas</font></font></span></b></li>
</ol>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Propriedades de pequeno e médio porte estão sujeitas a uma </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Isenção de Danos Acidentais não reembolsável,</font></font></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> que está incluída na taxa de reserva. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Destina-se a garantir aos hóspedes contra danos acidentais à propriedade até um valor de 250 € por reserva, mas exclui negligência ou vandalismo. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por qualquer dano que exceda 250 €, Smartavillas reserva-se o direito de lhe enviar uma fatura para pagamento imediato.</font></font></span></p>
<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start='2' type='i'>
 <li class='MsoNormal' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:justify;background:
     white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
     font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Villas e quintas grandes</font></font></span></b></li>
</ol>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Ao reservar nossas vilas maiores e exclusivas, um </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>depósito caução reembolsável de 500 €</font></font></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> será exigido. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Isso deve ser pago na chegada. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>O retorno deste depósito estará sujeito a uma inspeção e verificação satisfatórias do imóvel após a partida e será devolvido 14 dias antes da data de saída.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>d) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Hóspedes adicionais</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> -
 </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Para propriedades com instalações adicionais para dormir, como uma cama extra ocasional ou um sofá-cama, será cobrada uma taxa de </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>10 € por pessoa, por noite</font></font></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> . </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>As instalações de dormir para hóspedes adicionais serão listadas na descrição das instalações. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por exemplo, uma propriedade de 2 quartos pode aceitar 6 pessoas nos 2 quartos, mais 1 sofá-cama duplo.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>e) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Check-in tardio</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> 
- muitas de nossas propriedades possuem um cofre para chaves. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Para propriedades sem esta facilidade, um check-in pessoal tarde da noite será fornecido. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>As taxas cobradas por este serviço fora do horário normal serão de acordo com os seguintes horários e devem ser pagas no momento da chegada.</font></font></span></p>

  <p class='MsoNormal' align='center' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:center'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;

  <p class='MsoNormal' align='center' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:center'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;

  <p class='MsoNormal' align='center' style='margin-bottom:0cm;text-align:center'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;

<p class='MsoNormal'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:3.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;background:silver'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>* </font></font></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Crianças menores de 10 anos estão isentas.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>h) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Taxa de alteração</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> 
- uma vez confirmada a reserva, caso necessite de alguma alteração à mesma, </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>será cobrada </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>uma </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>taxa administrativa de 25 €</font></font></b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> . </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Para obter mais detalhes, consulte o </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Apêndice 1.</font></font></b></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>i) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Animais de estimação - nos casos em</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> que são permitidos animais de estimação, será cobrado um suplemento de 25 € à reserva. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por favor, verifique conosco com antecedência para garantir que os animais de estimação serão bem-vindos em sua propriedade alugada.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white;border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>3. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>CONFIRMANDO SUA RESERVA</font></font></span></b></p>
</div>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>a) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Detalhes da reserva -</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> você precisará preencher os detalhes de reserva necessários </font></font><b> </b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>para confirmá-la, os quais incluirão seus dados de contato, nomes e idades de todos os hóspedes e outras informações essenciais.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>b) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Pagamento</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Antes de fazer a reserva, você receberá um detalhamento de todos os custos associados à reserva, de acordo com suas necessidades e do imóvel alugado, juntamente com o cronograma de pagamento. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Você também receberá lembretes de pagamento para o pagamento do seu saldo.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>c) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Confirmação</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Assim que a reserva for confirmada enviaremos o endereço completo do seu imóvel alugado, instruções de viagem e outras informações importantes.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>d) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Antes de viajar</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:
10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Entraremos em contato novamente para confirmar os preparativos finais da viagem e responder a quaisquer perguntas finais que você possa ter sobre o check-in na propriedade alugada.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'></span></p>
<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white;border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>4. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>PAGAMENTO DA RESERVA</font></font></span></b></p>
</div>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Os termos de pagamento</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> , incluindo alterações e cancelamentos, estão descritos no </font></font><b><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Apêndice 1.</font></font></b></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>a) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Métodos de pagamento</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - Os pagamentos são exigidos na moeda indicada e devem ser pagos de acordo com o cronograma. </font><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Os pagamentos podem ser feitos das seguintes maneiras:</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:54.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-54.0pt;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>eu. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por cartão de débito / crédito usando nosso sistema automatizado</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:54.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-54.0pt;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>ii. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Por transferência bancária, com comprovativo de transferência a enviar por email</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:54.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-54.0pt;background:white'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>iii. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Para reservas tardias ou estadias prolongadas adicionais, pessoalmente no escritório com um cartão de crédito ou débito através de nosso terminal eletrônico</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;background:white'><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>b) </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;
color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>Taxas de transação</font></font></span></b><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'> - observe que é responsabilidade do hóspede / locatário pagar quaisquer taxas ou encargos associados cobrados por bancos ou instituições financeiras, por exemplo, transações de conversão de moeda de fora da UE.</font></font></span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='text-align:justify'><span lang='EN-US' style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
<div style='border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm;
background:white'>
<p class='MsoNormal' style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;background:white;vertical-align:baseline;
border:none;padding:0cm'><b><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>5. </font></font><span style='font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;'>&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif;color:black'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'><font style='vertical-align: inherit;'>TEMPOS DE CHECK-IN E CHECK-OUT</font></font></span></b></p>
</div>

line-height:115%;font-family:&quot;Century Gothic&quot;,sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
